GT Equivalence Verification (PO0)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(v) - omega0**c0*x**c1 - omega0**c2*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed):  
\[
-1.02670587028003\,x^3\;-\;1.02670587028003\,x\,e^{-|x|}\;+\;0.947981592038046\sin(t)\;-\;0.712276797350088\sin(v)
\]
So any matching candidate must be able (possibly after setting some candidate constants to 0) to represent **exactly**:
- an \(x^3\) term with coefficient \(-1.0267...\)
- an \(x\,e^{-|x|}\) term with coefficient \(-1.0267...\)
- a \(\sin(t)\) term with coefficient \(+0.94798...\) (cos allowed via phase shift)
- a \(-\sin(v)\) term with coefficient \(-0.71227...\)
and **no other dependence** on \(x,t,v\). Conditional equivalence can help only for things like \(|x|\) (e.g., assuming \(x\ge 0\) so \(|x|=x\)), but you still need the same functional forms.

Now check candidates:

1. Polynomial in \(x,v\) + cos(t). Has no \(x e^{-|x|}\) and no \(\sin(v)\) (only polynomial in \(v\)). Cannot match.
2. Has \(x^3\) and a \(t\)-dependent term \(e^{c7 t}\sin(c8 t+c9)\) (can reduce to \(\sin(t)\) by \(c7=0,c8=1\)). But no \(\sin(v)\) and no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
3. Same issue as (2): no \(\sin(v)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
4. Has \(e^{c2 x}\) and \(v^3,v\) (not \(\sin(v)\)), and no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
5. Same: \(e^{c2 x}\), linear \(v\), no \(\sin(v)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
6. Has \(x^3\) and a \(t\)-sin term, plus \(e^{c1/(c2+x)}\). No \(\sin(v)\). Also no way to make \(e^{c1/(c2+x)}\) become \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
7. Has \(e^{c2 x}\), \(v^3,v\), and separate \(e^{c6 t}\) and \(\sin(c8 t+c9)\). Still no \(\sin(v)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
8. Same: no \(\sin(v)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
9. Same: no \(\sin(v)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
10. Only \(x^2\), \(e^{c2 x}\), and \(t\)-sin. Missing \(x^3\), \(\sin(v)\), \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
11. Has \(x^3\) and \(\sin(t)\) term, but also \(x\cos(c5 t+c6)\) (cannot be removed unless \(c4=0\)), and no \(\sin(v)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
12. Has \(x^3\) and a mixed \(t\)-exp*sin(\(c8 x+c9\)) (depends on \(x\) inside sine), not allowed; also no \(\sin(v)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.

15. Has \(x^3\) and \(x\sin(t)\) (note extra factor \(x\)), plus polynomial in \(v\) and \(v|v|\). No \(\sin(v)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
